P. 75. L. 1.тАФThe answers given by the first four Ministers of Ar├нmardana to the question of their master, what is to be done with the captive Sthiraj├нvin are somewhat singular.Instead of stating how he is to be treated, they give lectures on the excellence of kindness, treachery, bribing and of the employment of force respectively, just as the ministers of Meghavarс╣Зa in the beginning of the book. These answers are, however, intended to indicate indirectly the manner how Sthiraj├нvin is to be used. Rakt├бksha, apparently, means to say, тАЬHear Sthiraj├нvin’sadvice; he spoke to his own master in favour of peace, and that is the right advice. Therefore treat him well and use him to make peace with thy enemy," (see line 5) while Kr├║r├бksha holds, that the captive is to be used to create discord in the enemy’s camp, D├нpt├бksha, that he is to bribe the opposite party and Vakran├бsa,that the war is to be continued and Sthiraj├нvin is to be killed without mercy.

P. 76. L. 13. тАФ R├бkshasa, originally the Minister of Nanda, became, after the death of the latter, the adviser of Malayaketu, the son of Parvatendra.
